    15→	ErrDuplicate         = errors.New("API key, organization ID and name must be unique")
    16→)

    28→	ServiceAccountId *int64       `db:"service_account_id"`
    29→	IsRevoked        *bool        `xorm:"is_revoked" db:"is_revoked"`
    30→}
    31→

    18→// timeNow makes it possible to test usage of time
    19→var timeNow = time.Now
    20→
    21→func (ss *sqlStore) GetAllAPIKeys(ctx context.Context, orgID int64) ([]*apikey.APIKey, error) {
    22→	result := make([]*apikey.APIKey, 0)
    23→	err := ss.db.WithDbSession(ctx, func(dbSession *db.Session) error {
    24→		sess := dbSession.Where("service_account_id IS NULL").Asc("name")
    25→		if orgID != -1 {
    26→			sess = sess.Where("org_id=?", orgID)
    27→		}
    28→		return sess.Find(&result)
    29→	})
    30→	return result, err
    31→}
    32→
    33→func (ss *sqlStore) AddAPIKey(ctx context.Context, cmd *apikey.AddCommand) (res *apikey.APIKey, err error) {
    34→	err = ss.db.WithTransactionalDbSession(ctx, func(sess *db.Session) error {
    35→		key := apikey.APIKey{OrgID: cmd.OrgID, Name: cmd.Name}
    36→		exists, _ := sess.Get(&key)
    37→		if exists {
    38→			return apikey.ErrDuplicate
    39→		}
    40→
    41→		updated := timeNow()
    42→		var expires *int64 = nil
    43→		if cmd.SecondsToLive > 0 {
    44→			v := updated.Add(time.Second * time.Duration(cmd.SecondsToLive)).Unix()
    45→			expires = &v
    46→		} else if cmd.SecondsToLive < 0 {
    47→			return apikey.ErrInvalidExpiration
    48→		}
    49→
    50→		isRevoked := false
    51→		t := apikey.APIKey{
    52→			OrgID:            cmd.OrgID,
    53→			Name:             cmd.Name,

type HTTPServer struct {
	log              log.Logger
	web              *web.Mux
	context          context.Context
	httpSrv          *http.Server
	middlewares      []web.Handler
	namedMiddlewares []routing.RegisterNamedMiddleware
	bus              bus.Bus

	pluginContextProvider        *plugincontext.Provider
	RouteRegister                routing.RouteRegister
--
		userVerifier:                 userVerifier,
	}
	if hs.Listener != nil {
		hs.log.Debug("Using provided listener")
	}
	hs.registerRoutes()

	// Register access control scope resolver for annotations
	hs.AccessControl.RegisterScopeAttributeResolver(AnnotationTypeScopeResolver(hs.annotationsRepo, features, dashboardService, folderService))

	if err := hs.declareFixedRoles(); err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}
	return hs, nil
}

func (hs *HTTPServer) AddMiddleware(middleware web.Handler) {
	hs.middlewares = append(hs.middlewares, middleware)
}

func (hs *HTTPServer) AddNamedMiddleware(middleware routing.RegisterNamedMiddleware) {
	hs.namedMiddlewares = append(hs.namedMiddlewares, middleware)
}

   102→func (h *ContextHandler) setRequestContext(ctx context.Context) context.Context {
   103→	ctx, span := tracing.Start(ctx, "ContextHandler.setRequestContext")
   104→	defer span.End()
   105→
   106→	reqContext := &contextmodel.ReqContext{
   107→		Context: web.FromContext(ctx),
   108→		SignedInUser: &user.SignedInUser{
   109→			Permissions: map[int64]map[string][]string{},
   110→		},
   111→		IsSignedIn:                false,
   112→		AllowAnonymous:            false,
   113→		SkipDSCache:               false,
   114→		Logger:                    log.New("context"),
   115→		UseSessionStorageRedirect: h.features.IsEnabledGlobally(featuremgmt.FlagUseSessionStorageForRedirection),
   116→	}
   117→
   118→	// inject ReqContext in the context
   119→	ctx = context.WithValue(ctx, reqContextKey{}, reqContext)
   120→	// store list of possible auth header in context
   121→	ctx = WithAuthHTTPHeaders(ctx, h.cfg)
   122→	// Set the context for the http.Request.Context
   123→	// This modifies both r and reqContext.Req since they point to the same value
   124→	*reqContext.Req = *reqContext.Req.WithContext(ctx)
   125→
   126→	traceID := tracing.TraceIDFromContext(ctx, false)
   127→	if traceID != "" {
   128→		reqContext.Logger = reqContext.Logger.New("traceID", traceID)
   129→	}
   130→
   131→	id, err := h.authenticator.Authenticate(ctx, &authn.Request{HTTPRequest: reqContext.Req})
   132→	if err != nil {
   133→		// Hack: set all errors on LookupTokenErr, so we can check it in auth middlewares
   134→		reqContext.LookupTokenErr = err
   135→	} else {
   136→		reqContext.SignedInUser = id.SignedInUser()
   137→		reqContext.UserToken = id.SessionToken
   138→		reqContext.IsSignedIn = !reqContext.IsAnonymous
   139→		reqContext.AllowAnonymous = reqCon
... (truncated)

   106→
   107→func (s *Service) Authenticate(ctx context.Context, r *authn.Request) (*authn.Identity, error) {
   108→	ctx, span := s.tracer.Start(ctx, "authn.Authenticate")
   109→	defer span.End()
   110→
   111→	orgID, err := s.orgIDFromRequest(r)
   112→	if err != nil {
   113→		return nil, err
   114→	}
   115→	r.OrgID = orgID
   116→
   117→	var authErr error
   118→	for _, item := range s.clientQueue.items {
   119→		if item.v.Test(ctx, r) {
   120→			identity, err := s.authenticate(ctx, item.v, r)
   121→			if err != nil {
   122→				// Note: special case for token rotation
   123→				// We don't want to fallthrough in this case
   124→				if errors.Is(err, authn.ErrTokenNeedsRotation) {
   125→					return nil, err
   126→				}
   127→
   128→				authErr = errors.Join(authErr, err)
   129→				// try next
   130→				continue
   131→			}
   132→
   133→			if identity != nil {
   134→				s.metrics.successfulAuth.WithLabelValues(item.v.Name()).Inc()
   135→				return identity, nil
   136→			}
   137→		}
   138→	}
   139→
   140→	if authErr != nil {
   141→		s.metrics.failedAuth.Inc()
   142→		return nil, authErr
   143→	}
   144→
   145→	return nil, errCantAuthenticateReq.Errorf("cannot authenticate request")
   146→}

   103→func (ss *sqlStore) UpdateAPIKeyLastUsedDate(ctx context.Context, tokenID int64) error {
   104→	now := timeNow()

   108→		}

   111→	})

   114→func (ss *sqlStore) Count(ctx context.Context, scopeParams *quota.ScopeParameters) (*quota.Map, error) {
   115→	u := &quota.Map{}
   116→	type result struct {
   117→		Count int64
   118→	}
   119→
   120→	r := result{}
   121→	if err := ss.db.WithDbSession(ctx, func(sess *sqlstore.DBSession) error {
   122→		rawSQL := "SELECT COUNT(*) AS count FROM api_key"
   123→		if _, err := sess.SQL(rawSQL).Get(&r); err != nil {
   124→			return err
   125→		}
   126→		return nil
   127→	}); err != nil {
   128→		return u, err
   129→	} else {
   130→		tag, err := quota.NewTag(apikey.QuotaTargetSrv, apikey.QuotaTarget, quota.GlobalScope)
   131→		if err != nil {
   132→			return nil, err
   133→		}
   134→		u.Set(tag, r.Count)
   135→	}
   136→
   137→	if scopeParams != nil && scopeParams.OrgID != 0 {
   138→		if err := ss.db.WithDbSession(ctx, func(sess *sqlstore.DBSession) error {
   139→			rawSQL := "SELECT COUNT(*) AS count FROM api_key WHERE org_id = ?"
   140→			if _, err := sess.SQL(rawSQL, scopeParams.OrgID).Get(&r); err != nil {
   141→				return err
   142→			}
   143→			return nil
   144→		}); err != nil {
   145→			return u, err
   146→		} else {
   147→			tag, err := quota.NewTag(apikey.QuotaTargetSrv, apikey.QuotaTarget, quota.OrgScope)
   148→			if err != nil {
   149→				return nil, err
   150→			}

    11→type KeyGenResult struct {
    12→	HashedKey    string
    13→	ClientSecret string
    14→}
    15→
    16→type ApiKeyJson struct {
    17→	Key   string `json:"k"`
    18→	Name  string `json:"n"`
    19→	OrgId int64  `json:"id"`
    20→}
    21→
    22→func New(orgId int64, name string) (KeyGenResult, error) {
    23→	result := KeyGenResult{}
    24→
    25→	jsonKey := ApiKeyJson{}
    26→	jsonKey.OrgId = orgId
    27→	jsonKey.Name = name
    28→	var err error
    29→	jsonKey.Key, err = util.GetRandomString(32)
    30→	if err != nil {
    31→		return result, err
    32→	}
    33→
    34→	result.HashedKey, err = util.EncodePassword(jsonKey.Key, name)
    35→	if err != nil {
    36→		return result, err
    37→	}
    38→
    39→	jsonString, err := json.Marshal(jsonKey)
    40→	if err != nil {
    41→		return result, err
    42→	}
    43→
    44→	result.ClientSecret = base64.StdEncoding.EncodeToString(jsonString)
    45→	return result, nil
    46→}
    47→
    48→func Decode(keyString string) (*ApiKeyJson, error) {
    49→	jsonString, err := base64.StdEncoding.DecodeString(keyString)
    50→	if err != nil {
    51→		return nil, satokengen.ErrInvalidApiKey
    52→	}
    53→
    54→	var keyObj ApiKeyJson
    55→	err = json.Unmarshal(jsonString, &keyObj)
    56→	if err != nil {
    57→		return nil, satokengen.ErrInvalidApiKey
    58→	}
    59→
    60→	return &keyObj, nil
    61→}

    22→	ServiceID string
    23→	Secret    string
    24→	Checksum  string
    25→}
    26→
    27→func (p *PrefixedKey) Hash() (string, error) {
    28→	hash, err := util.EncodePassword(p.Secret, p.Checksum)
    29→	if err != nil {
    30→		return "", err
    31→	}
    32→	return hash, nil
    33→}
    34→
    35→func (p *PrefixedKey) key() string {
    36→	return GrafanaPrefix + p.ServiceID + "_" + p.Secret
    37→}
    38→
    39→func (p *PrefixedKey) CalculateChecksum() string {
    40→	checksum := crc32.ChecksumIEEE([]byte(p.key()))
    41→	//checksum to []byte
    42→	checksumBytes := make([]byte, 4)
    43→	checksumBytes[0] = byte(checksum)
    44→	checksumBytes[1] = byte(checksum >> 8)
    45→	checksumBytes[2] = byte(checksum >> 16)
    46→	checksumBytes[3] = byte(checksum >> 24)
    47→
    48→	return hex.EncodeToString(checksumBytes)
    49→}
    50→
    51→func (p *PrefixedKey) String() string {
    52→	return p.key() + "_" + p.Checksum
    53→}
    54→

    60→		return result, err
    61→	}
    62→
    63→	key := PrefixedKey{ServiceID: serviceID, Secret: secret, Checksum: ""}
    64→	key.Checksum = key.CalculateChecksum()
    65→
    66→	result.Hashe

4. **Service account binding** - Requiring ServiceAccountId linkage
5. **Role-based access** - Using key.Role as DefaultOrgRole for permissions

scope enforcement through a layered architecture spanning multiple services. The authentication flow begins in the HTTP middleware stack where ContextHandler (pkg/services/contexthandler/contexthandler.go) acts as the entry point, calling the Authenticator service to process incoming requests. The ContextHandler.Middleware initializes a ReqContext and invokes authn.Service.Authenticate with an authn.Request containing the HTTP request details.\\n\\nThe authentication service (pkg/services/authn/authnimpl/service.go) orchestrates multiple authentication clients in priority order, including the APIKey client. When the APIKey client (pkg/services/authn/clients/api_key.go) detects an API key in the Authorization header (either as Bearer token or Basic auth with 'api_key' username), it attempts authentication. The client retrieves the API key from the database using either the modern service account token format handled by satokengen (pkg/components/satokengen/tokengen.go) or the legacy format handled by apikeygen (pkg/components/apikeygen/apikeygen.go).\\n\\nAPI key validation occurs in the validateApiKey function (pkg/services/authn/clients/api_key.go), which enforces three critical security checks: expiration validation (comparing key.Expires timestamp against current time), revocation status checking (key.IsRevoked flag), and organization scope enforcement (verifying key.OrgID matches the requested organization). Additionally, the client enforces that API keys must be associated with a service account (key.ServiceAccountId must be non-null).\\n\\nThe API key model (pkg/services/apikey/model.go) contains fields for: Expires (optional timestamp for expiration), IsRevoked (optional boolean flag), ServiceAccountId (links to service account), and Role (organization role type). The APIKey service implementation (pkg/services/apikey/apikeyimpl/apikey.go) provides the Service interface that includes GetAPIKeyByHash, GetApiKeyByName, AddAPIKey, and UpdateAPIKeyLastUsedDate methods. The underlying SQL store (pkg/services/apikey/apikeyimpl/xorm_store.go) implements database operations including quota scoping with OrgScope and GlobalScope parameters.\\n\\nScope enforcement extends beyond the API key itself through the Identity system. The validateApiKey function checks organization membership, and the resulting Identity object created by newServiceAccountIdentity function contains OrgID for scope isolation. The service account's DefaultOrgRole (set from key.Role in pkg/services/serviceaccounts/database/store.go) determines permission scope. The Identity struct (pkg/services/authn/identity.go) maintains OrgRoles mapping organization IDs to role types, enabling fine-grained access control evaluation through the AccessControl service (pkg/services/accesscontrol/accesscontrol.go).\\n\\nPost-authentication, the Hook method (pkg/services/authn/clients/api_key.go) asynchronously updates the LastUsedAt timestamp in the api_key table, providing audit capabilities for API key usage tracking. The complete authentication chain flows from HTTP middleware through the authenticator service, API key client, database retrieval, validation checks, scope enforcement, and finally identity creation for downstream authorization decisions.\"\n}\n",
